@100348 = ~Set Snare
Set a trap in the chosen location when no hostile creatures are in sight. Traps grow more powerful with the character's level and can only be triggered by enemies.
  1st Level: Deals 2d8+5 missile damage.
  11th Level: Deals 2d8+5 missile damage, plus 2d6 poison damage per round for the next 3 rounds.
  16th Level: Deals 3d8+5 missile damage, plus 4d8+2 fire damage.
  21st Level: Deals 3d8+5 missile damage and 20 poison damage with no save; slays target if a Save vs. Death with a +4 bonus is failed.《裝設陷阱
當視野中無敵對生物時在選定位置設置一個陷阱。陷阱隨人物等級加強且只能被敵人觸發。
–1級：造成2d8+5遠程傷害。
–11級：造成2d8+5遠程傷害，並額外在接下3輪造成每輪2d6毒素傷害。
–16級：造成3d8+5遠程傷害和4d8+2火焰傷害。
–21級：造成3d8+5遠程傷害和20無豁免毒素傷害；如果目標以+4有利通過對死亡的豁免鑒定失敗則立刻死亡。》~
@100349 = ~Set Special Snare
Set a trap in the chosen location when no hostile creatures are in sight. Traps grow more powerful with the character's level and can only be triggered by enemies.
  1st Level: Deals 3d8+5 missile damage and slows target for 5 rounds if a Save vs. Spell with a -4 penalty is failed.
  11th Level: Deals 4d8+5 missile damage and holds target for 5 rounds if a Save vs. Spell with a -1 penalty is failed.
  16th Level: Erects an Otiluke's Resilient Sphere around the target for 7 rounds if a Save vs. Spell is failed.
  21st Level: Mazes the target.《裝設特殊陷阱
當視野中無敵對生物時在選定位置設置一個陷阱。陷阱隨人物升級加強且只能被敵人觸發。
–1級：造成3d8+5遠程傷害，如目標未能以-4不利通過對法術的豁免檢定則被減速5輪。
–11級：造成4d8+5遠程傷害，如目標未能以-1不利通過對法術的豁免檢定則被定身5輪。
–16級：如目標未能通過對法術的豁免檢定，則在目標周圍產生一個持續7輪的歐提路克彈力護罩。
–21級：目標受迷宮效果影響。》~

日魂武僧將體內的光明之力導向徒手攻擊，令雙拳變為可在下一輪造成2d6額外火焰傷害的燃燒武器。效果持續時間將在等級9時增加至2輪，在等級12時增加至3輪，在等級15時增加至4輪，在等級25時增加至5輪。該特殊能力自動修正普通攻擊，無需切換武器。》~
@100356 = ~Charm Animal
This spell affects any single animal it is cast upon. The animal is allowed a Saving Throw vs. Spell to negate the effect.

If the spell's recipient fails its Saving Throw, it regards the caster as a trusted friend and ally to be heeded and protected. The caster may give it orders, and the charmed animal will carry them out as quickly as possible.

If the caster harms—or attempts to harm—the charmed animal by some overt action, or if a Dispel Magic spell is cast upon the charmed animal, the Charm spell is broken. If two or more Charms simultaneously affect a creature, the most recent Charm takes precedence. Note that the subject will be hostile when the Charm expires, regardless of its original attitude. Also note that you cannot have a charmed creature leave the area where it was charmed.《魅惑動物
這個法術影響單個動物，該動物如通過對法術的豁免鑒定可避免被魅惑，否則將把施法者視為要聽從和保護的可信朋友和夥伴。施法者可以向它下令，而被魅惑動物會盡可能快地執行它們。

如果施法者傷害——或是明顯企圖傷害——被魅惑動物，或是被魅惑的動物被解除魔法，魅惑效果將結束。如果兩個或更多魅惑效果同時影響同一個生物，則最後施放的魅惑生效。注意當魅惑結束時受術者可能變得敵對，無論它原本的態度是否敵對。此外，被魅惑的動物無法離開它所在的區域。》~

@100358 = ~Aura of Despair
Targets all enemies within 15 ft. with effects that improve based on the caster's level:
  3rd Level: -1 penalty to hit and damage rolls and a -2 penalty to Armor Class for 1 turn.
  6th Level: -2 penalty to hit and damage rolls and a -2 penalty to Armor Class for 1 turn.
  15th Level: All enemies suffer a -4 penalty to hit and damage rolls and a -4 penalty to Armor Class for 1 turn; enemies with 8 or fewer Hit Dice are panicked as well.
  20th Level: All enemies suffer a -4 penalty to hit and damage rolls and a -4 penalty to Armor Class for 1 turn; enemies with 18 or fewer Hit Dice are panicked as well.
There is no Saving Throw against this ability.《絕望光環
自身30呎內的敵人都將受到以下效果影響，具體取決於施法者的等級（無豁免）：
–3級：命中和傷害-1不利，防禦等級-2不利，持續1回合。
–6級：命中和傷害-2不利，防禦等級-2不利，持續1回合。
–15級：命中和傷害-4不利，防禦等級-4不利，持續1回合；對於等級8及以下的敵人造成恐懼效果。
–20級：命中和傷害-4不利，防禦等級-4不利，持續1回合；對於等級18及以下的敵人造成恐懼效果。》~

After the effects end, the character becomes winded, suffering a -2 penalty to Armor Class, to-hit rolls, and damage rolls.《狂暴

@101640 = ~Shadow Twin《陰影雙子》~
@101641 = ~Shadow Twin
This ability creates an almost exact duplicate of the Shadowdancer for 2 turns. The duplicate is created at 60% of the level at which the Shadowdancer is currently on. It has all the abilities that the Shadowdancer would have at that level. It also has 60% of the Hit Points of the Shadowdancer. The duplicate is fully under the control of the Shadowdancer.《陰影雙子
此能力產生一個持續2輪，幾乎與影舞者一模一樣的複製品。複製品產生後的等級為影舞者當前等級的60%。它擁有該等級下影舞者的所有能力。它也擁有影舞者60%的生命值。複製品完全處於影舞者的控制下。》~
@101642 = ~Shadow Form《影之形》~
@101643 = ~Shadow Form
This ability temporarily transposes some of the user's tissue with shadow-material, making the subject partially incorporeal. For the next 5 rounds, all physical attacks directed against the Shadowdancer only deal 50% of their normal damage. During this time, the Shadowdancer is also under the effects of Improved Invisibility and cannot be directly targeted by spells.《影之形
該能力暫時將使用者的部分群組織轉換為陰影物質，使其部分無形。在接下來的5輪內，所有對影舞者的物理攻擊只能造成通常傷害的50%。在此期間影舞者也處於高級隱身狀態下，無法被法術直接瞄準。》~

@101645 = ~Shadow Maze

@102780 = ~Domination

Range: Visual range of the vampire
Duration: 8 rounds 
Casting Time: 1 
Area of Effect: 1 creature 
Saving Throw: Neg.

A vampire's mental abilities are powerful tools indeed. Domination enables the vampire to control the actions of any creature while the ability is in effect. This control is maintained through a telepathic link between the caster and the victim. Unlike the 4th-level priest spell Mental Domination, the target has no option for release, even if made to do something against their morals. This effect can only be reversed by Dispel Magic. The target is allowed a Saving Throw vs. Spell with a -2 penalty to negate the effect.《控制術

有效距離：吸血鬼視線所及
持續時間：8輪
施法時間：1
影響範圍：一個生物
豁免檢定：通過則無效

吸血鬼的精神能力的確是強大的工具。控制術可以讓吸血鬼在能力生效期間控制任何生物的行動。這種控制通過施法者和受術者之間的心靈鏈接進行維持。和四級的牧師神術心智控制不同，目標沒有被釋放的可能，即使是被命令做和他們不願意的事情。這個效果只能被解除魔法所移除。目標需要以-2不利通過對法術的豁免檢定才能免受該效果影響。》~

@103001 = ~Mirror Image
(Illusion/Phantasm)

Level: 2
Range: 0
Duration: 15 rounds
Casting Time: 1
Area of Effect: Special
Saving Throw: None

Cerebus creates 6 exact duplicates of himself. These images do exactly what he does. Since the spell causes a blurring and slight distortion when cast, it is impossible for opponents to be certain which are the illusions and which is the actual Cerebus. When an image is struck by a melee or missile attack—magical or otherwise—it disappears, but any other existing images remain intact until they are struck. However, it is important to note that this will not protect Cerebus against every attack, as it is possible for an enemy to choose the real one amongst all the images.《鏡影術
（幻術系/魅影系）

等級：2
有效距離：0
持續時間：15輪
施法時間：1
影響範圍：特殊
豁免檢定：無

瑟裡布斯創造出自己的6個精確的複製影像。這些影像和他的行動完全一樣。這個法術在施展時會造成模糊和輕微的扭曲，因此對手不可能確定哪個是鏡像、哪個是真正的瑟裡布斯。當一個影像遭受近戰或遠程攻擊——無論是魔法還是別的——它會消失，但其它所有的影像會繼續存在，直到它們都被擊中為止。然而，需要注意的是這個能力並不能保護瑟裡布斯免受每次攻擊的傷害，因為敵人還是有可能從所有影像中選中本體。》~

@103007 = ~Dispel Magic
(Abjuration)

Level: 1
Range: 40 ft.
Duration: Instant
Casting Time: 1
Area of Effect: 15-ft. radius
Saving Throw: None

A Dispel Magic spell removes magical effects upon anyone within the area. This includes effects given from spells, potions and certain magical items such as wands. It does not, however, affect enchanted magical items or spell protections such as Spell Turning and Spell Deflection. The chance of the dispel succeeding is determined by the level of the caster and the level of the magic being dispelled. The base chance of successfully dispelling is 50%. For every level that the caster of the Dispel Magic is above the original caster, <PRO_HISHER> chance of success increases by 5%. For every level that the caster of Dispel Magic is below the original caster, <PRO_HISHER> chance of success decreases by 10%. However, despite the difference in levels, there is always at least a 5% chance of success or failure. Thus, if a caster is 10 levels higher than the magic <PRO_HESHE> is trying to dispel, there is only a 5% chance of failure. Similarly if the caster is 4 levels lower than the magic <PRO_HESHE> is trying to dispel, there is only a 10% chance of success. Intuitively, this spell is almost useless if the target is 5 or more levels higher than the caster.

Note: While this spell dispels the individual effects of Grease, Web, Stinking Cloud, and other such spells, it does not dispel the area of effect.《解除魔法
（防護系）

等級：1
有效距離：40呎
持續時間：立即
施法時間：1
影響範圍：半徑30呎
豁免檢定：無

解除魔法術可以將作用範圍內所有人身上的魔法效果除去，包括法術、藥水，或是諸如法杖等魔法物品的影響；但是它並不會影響到魔法物品本身的效力，或是法術反轉與法術偏轉等防護法術的效力。解除魔法的成功機率，取決於施法者本身的等級以及施展目標法術者的等級。此法術的基本成功機率為50%，倘若解除法術的施法者等級高於目標法術的施法者等級，每高一級移除法術的成功機率便會增加	5%。然而若是施法者的等級低於原施術者，那麼成功的機率便會每低一級降低10%。但不論等級相差多少，至少一定會有	5%的成功或失敗機率。因此如果施法者的等級高上十級，便只有	5%的失敗機會；但相對的，如果施法者的等級低上四級，那麼便只有10%的機會可以成功解除對手的魔法。很顯然地，只要對方施法者的等級高於己方五級或以上，這法術就幾乎等於沒有用處。

注意：雖然這法術能夠移除個體身上所遭受的油膩術、蛛網術、臭雲術等法術的效果，但是卻無法消除這些法術的區域性效果。》~
@103008 = ~Find Familiar
(Conjuration/Summoning)

Level: 1
Range: 0
Duration: Permanent
Casting Time: 1
Area of Effect: Special
Saving Throw: None

This spell enables the Beast Master to attempt to summon a familiar to act as <PRO_HISHER> aide and companion. Familiars are typically small creatures. A creature acting as a familiar can benefit its master, conveying its sensory powers to <PRO_HIMHER>, conversing with <PRO_HIMHER>, and serving as a guard/scout/spy as well. A Beast Master can have only one familiar at a time, and <PRO_HESHE> has no control over what sort of creature answers the summoning, if any come at all.

Note: This spell can only be cast by the protagonist.

The creature is always more intelligent than others of its type (typically by 2 or 3 Intelligence points), and its bond with the Beast Master confers upon it an exceptionally long life. The Beast Master has an empathic link with the familiar and can issue it mental commands. The Beast Master receives half the familiar's total Hit Points (rounded down) as bonus Hit Points. However, the Beast Master must take care to treat <PRO_HISHER> familiar well, for if the familiar should die, the Beast Master loses the bonus Hit Points and the familiar's Hit Points again as damage. Also, when a familiar dies, the Beast Master loses 1 point of Constitution PERMANENTLY.

Example: A Beast Master has 10 Hit Points and casts Find Familiar. The fairy dragon summoned has 24 Hit Points, so the Beast Master gets a bonus of 12 Hit Points. The Beast Master now has 22 Hit Points. If the familiar dies, the Beast Master loses those 12 Hit Points (putting <PRO_HIMHER> back at 10), loses 1 point of Constitution permanently (which may cause additional Hit Point loss), and takes 24 damage.

Here is a list of the familiars that the Beast Master receives according to alignment:

LAWFUL GOOD, NEUTRAL GOOD: Pseudo Dragon
– Hit Points: 24
– Armor Class: -2
– Magic Resistance: 50%
– Combat: 2 attacks per round at 13 THAC0 for 1d3 damage, save vs. Death or be rendered unconscious for 2 turns
– Special Abilities: Can cast Blur once per day. Regenerates 1 HP/round. Immune to level drain, sleep, and petrification.

CHAOTIC GOOD: Fairy Dragon
– Hit Points: 24
– Armor Class: 4
– Magic Resistance: 32%
– Combat: 2 attacks per round at 13 THAC0 for 1d2 damage
– Special Abilities: Can cast Mirror Image and Invisibility, 10' Radius once per day. Immune to level drain, sleep, and petrification.《尋找魔寵
（咒法系／召喚系）

豁免檢定：無

此法術可讓馴獸師試圖尋找一名魔寵，做為<PRO_HISHER>幫手或同伴。這些魔寵一般而言都是小型生物。魔寵生物能為主人帶來一些好處，增強<PRO_HIMHER>感知力、與<PRO_HIMHER>交談或是扮演護衛、偵查或間諜等角色。馴獸師一次只能有一名魔寵，而且<PRO_HIMHER>也無法控制何種生物回應召喚，如果有的話。

注意：只有主角可以施展尋找魔寵這個法術。

被召喚的生物往往比其同類生物更聰明（高2-3點的智力），而與馴獸師的羈絆也使其壽命延長。馴獸師會與這名魔寵心靈相通，因而可藉由心靈傳達命令。馴獸師亦可獲得魔寵生命值的一半（向下取整），作為自己額外的生命點數。不過，馴獸師必須善待<PRO_HISHER>魔寵，否則一旦魔寵死亡，馴獸師將喪失增加的額外生命值，以及損失一半的魔寵生命值（等同於傷害）。而且，魔寵的死也將使馴獸師「永遠」失去1點的體質屬性。

舉例說明：一名擁有10點生命值的馴獸師施展尋找魔寵。受召喚的妖精龍有24點生命值，因此馴獸師獲得12點的生命值獎勵，現在他擁有22點生命值。如果妖精龍死亡，馴獸師喪失12點生命值（回到<PRO_HISHER>原本的10點）、永久失去1點的體質（可能會因此而損失更多生命值），並且受到12點傷害。

這是依據陣營可能獲得的魔寵清單：

守序善良、中立善良：偽龍
-生命值：24
-防禦等級：-2
-魔法抗性：50﹪
-戰鬥能力：每輪以13零級命中值攻擊2次，每擊1d3點傷害。被擊中的對象必須對死亡進行豁免檢定，否則將昏迷2回合。
-特殊能力：每天可以施展1次朦朧術。每輪恢復1點生命值。免疫等級吸取、睡眠和石化。

混亂善良：妖精龍
-生命值：24
-防禦等級：4
-魔法抗性：32﹪
-戰鬥能力：每輪可攻擊2次，攻擊的零級命中值為13，可造成1d2點傷害。
-特殊能力：每天可以施展1次鏡影術、隱形術和10呎隱形術。免疫等級吸取、睡眠和石化。》~

@103045 = "~Note di Traduzione~

Gli Allegri Buffoni stanno lavorando all'aggiornamento della traduzione vanilla di Baldur's Gate 2 (Shadows of Amn e Throne of Bhaal). Considerata la significativa mole di testi, è un impegno che richiederà parecchio tempo, ma il gruppo è determinato a cesellare questa traduzione, portandola ai livelli di qualità di Baldur's Gate: Enhanced Edition e Icewind Dale: Enhanced Edition.
A tale scopo, invitiamo tutti i giocatori a segnalare qualsiasi refuso nel thread dedicato nella sezione italiana di forums.beamdog.com.

Tutti gli elementi relativi all'universo di Dungeons & Dragons e all'Ambientazione Forgotten Realms, fra cui incantesimi, specializzazioni, classi, sottoclassi, abilità, oggetti, luoghi e personaggi, sono stati tradotti in italiano secondo la terminologia ufficiale adottata nei manuali di Advanced Dungeons & Dragons Seconda Edizione. Segue l'elenco del materiale principale di supporto:

Edizioni Twenty-Five Editions:
Manuale del Giocatore * Manuale del Dungeon Master
Manuale dei Mostri Volume I e II * Abilità e Poteri
Combattimento e Tattiche * Incantesimi e Magia
Dar Vita ai Reami * A Spasso per i Reami

Edizioni Ripa:
Manuale del Dungeon Master * Manuale dei Mostri

Data la mancata localizzazione italiana di numerosi manuali Advanced, il team si è dovuto avvalere delle successive pubblicazioni di Dungeons & Dragons Terza Edizione (3.0/3.5 Twenty-Five Editions) nel pieno rispetto delle fonti canoniche. Segue l'elenco dell'ulteriore materiale:

Forgotten Realms Ambientazione * Razze di Faerûn
Magia di Faerûn * Signori dell'Oscurità
Splendente Sud * Imperi Perduti di Faerûn
Irraggiungibile Est * Marche d'Argento
Fedi e Pantheon * Manuale del Giocatore
Guida del Dungeon Master * Manuale dei Mostri
Manuale dei Mostri II * Manuale dei Piani
Atlante Planare

In ogni altro caso, come nei termini senza precedenti, la trasposizione in italiano ha cercato di essere il più fedele possibile all'originale inglese.《~Note di Traduzione~

Gli Allegri Buffoni stanno lavorando all'aggiornamento della traduzione vanilla di Baldur's Gate 2 (Shadows of Amn e Throne of Bhaal). Considerata la significativa mole di testi, e un impegno che richiedera parecchio tempo, ma il gruppo e determinato a cesellare questa traduzione, portandola ai livelli di qualita di Baldur's Gate: Enhanced Edition e Icewind Dale: Enhanced Edition.
A tale scopo, invitiamo tutti i giocatori a segnalare qualsiasi refuso nel thread dedicato nella sezione italiana di forums.beamdog.com.

Tutti gli elementi relativi all'universo di Dungeons & Dragons e all'Ambientazione Forgotten Realms, fra cui incantesimi, specializzazioni, classi, sottoclassi, abilita, oggetti, luoghi e personaggi, sono stati tradotti in italiano secondo la terminologia ufficiale adottata nei manuali di Advanced Dungeons & Dragons Seconda Edizione. Segue l'elenco del materiale principale di supporto:

Edizioni Ripa:
Manuale del Dungeon Master * Manuale dei Mostri

Data la mancata localizzazione italiana di numerosi manuali Advanced, il team si e dovuto avvalere delle successive pubblicazioni di Dungeons & Dragons Terza Edizione (3.0/3.5 Twenty-Five Editions) nel pieno rispetto delle fonti canoniche. Segue l'elenco dell'ulteriore materiale:

Forgotten Realms Ambientazione * Razze di Faerun
Magia di Faerun * Signori dell'Oscurita
Splendente Sud * Imperi Perduti di Faerun
Irraggiungibile Est * Marche d'Argento
Fedi e Pantheon * Manuale del Giocatore
Guida del Dungeon Master * Manuale dei Mostri
Manuale dei Mostri II * Manuale dei Piani
Atlante Planare

In ogni altro caso, come nei termini senza precedenti, la trasposizione in italiano ha cercato di essere il piu fedele possibile all'originale inglese.》"

While doing so would be understandable, it would also be wasteful, at least if their creator is to be believed. He claimed that consuming a single dumpling before a battle would lend the eater additional vigor; from his tone, you infer that eating all in one sitting would give you indigestion.

STATISTICS:

THAC0: +1
Duration: 1 turn

Weight: 0《這些散發出令人垂涎香氣的美味糰子讓人忍不住一口全吞下去。雖然這麼做可以理解，但也很浪費，至少做餃子的人是這麼認為的。他宣稱只要在戰鬥前吃上一顆就能夠獲得額外的活力；根據他的說法你猜想一次全部吃完恐怕會消化不良。

@103059 = ~shaman《薩滿》~
@103060 = ~SHAMAN: Shamans forge a divine connection with the natural world, similar to the way Druids commune with nature, but Shamans are more spiritual than primal. They directly tap into the energies that flow through the earth and air, through plants and animals, and even through the dead, and shape these energies to obey their will. Nowhere is this more evident than in their ability to summon powerful spirits as guardians and defenders. A being of two worlds, Shamans value balance over dominance.

CLASS FEATURES:

– May only wear leather, studded leather, and hide armor.
– May not equip shields larger than bucklers.
– May only use the following weapons: dagger, club, spear, axe, quarterstaff, dart, sling, and shortbow.
– May only become Proficient (one slot) in any weapon class.
– May only become Proficient (one slot) in any fighting style.
– May cast druidic spells.
– Does not automatically learn all spells of a given level as Druids do. Instead, Shamans select new spells to learn at each level, which they can cast daily without memorization.
– Gains immediate access to a number of Shaman-specific spells, which can be cast like any other: Spirit Ward, Writhing Fog, Spiritual Clarity, Spirit Fire, Recall Spirit, Spiritual Lock, and Ether Gate.
– Gains use of the Detect Illusion skill with 20% points as a base and an 4 points per level, up to a maximum of 100% at level 20.
– May use Shamanic Dance at will.

SHAMANIC DANCE: Shamans can summon spirit allies by performing a ritualistic dance. While dancing, the Shaman takes a -4 penalty to Armor Class and cannot move, attack, cast spells, use items and special abilities, or perform any other activity. Each round while the Shaman dances, there is a 35% base chance plus 2% for each level of the Shaman that a spirit will answer the call, up to a maximum of 75% at level 20. Any summoned spirits will disappear if the Shaman moves, stops dancing, or if the spirits leave visual range. The spirits grow in power as the Shaman gains additional levels:
  Level 1: Minor animal spirits (snake, fox, hound), up to 2 spirits at the same time.
  Level 6: Major animal spirits (bear, panther, boar), up to 3 spirits at the same time.
  Level 12: Minor nature spirits (lesser air spirit, lesser earth spirit, lesser fire spirit), up to 4 spirits at the same time.
  Level 18: Major nature spirits (air spirit, earth spirit, fire spirit), up to 5 spirits at the same time.
The type of the summoned spirit is randomly determined from all the spirits available at the Shaman's level. For example, a level 12 Shaman will summon either a minor nature spirit, a major animal spirit, or a minor animal spirit, but cannot choose which one appears. Spirits will do their best to protect the Shaman but are not controlled directly.

– Does not gain bonus spells per day from high Wisdom.
– Alignment restricted to neutral good, true neutral, and neutral evil.
– Ineligible for any stronghold.
– Hit Die: d8《薩滿：薩滿鍛造出一條神聖的通道與自然界進行連接，類似德魯伊與自然交談的方法，但要比這種原始的交談更加宗教化。他們直接利用流淌在大地與空氣，植物和動物，甚至死屍中的能量，對這些能量進行塑形，讓能量遵循他們的意志。顯而易見地，他們的能力可以召喚強大的靈魂作為守護者和防禦者。作為行走於兩個世界的存在，薩滿注重平衡而不是支配。

職業特點：

–只能穿著皮甲、皮環甲和厚皮甲
–無法裝備比小圓盾更大型的盾牌
–只能使用下列武器：匕首、棍棒、長矛、斧、手杖、飛鏢、投石索和短弓
–對任何武器種類都只能熟練掌握（1星）
–對任何武器模式都只能熟練掌握（1星）
–可以施展德魯伊法術
–不能像德魯伊那樣自動學會每個等級的所有法術，而是在升級時可以選擇新的法術進行學習。他們不需要記憶就可以每天施展這些法術
–立即獲取一系列薩滿獨有的法術，可以像其它法術一樣施展：靈魂守護，痛苦迷霧，靈魂清淨，靈魂火焰，靈魂召還，靈魂封鎖，以及以太之門
–獲得偵測幻象的能力，初始20點，每等級提升4點，最高在20級達到100點
–生命骰：D8
–可以任意施展薩滿舞

	薩滿舞：薩滿可以進行一場儀式舞蹈來召喚靈魂盟友。在舞蹈中，薩滿的AC-4不利且無法移動、攻擊、施法、使用物品和特殊能力，以及進行任何其它動作。在舞蹈中每輪有35%的基礎概率使一個靈魂回應薩滿的召喚，且每個薩滿等級提升2%概率，最高在20級達到75%。如果薩滿移動或停止舞蹈就會令召喚的靈魂消失，靈魂距離太遠離開視線也會消失。靈魂會隨著薩滿達到特定等級而增強：
		等級1：小型動物靈（蛇，狐狸，獵狗），同時最多存在兩個靈魂。
		等級6：大型動物靈（熊，獵豹，野豬），同時最多存在三個靈魂。
		等級12：小型自然靈（小型風靈，小型土靈，小型火靈），同時最多存在四個靈魂。
		等級18：大型自然靈（風靈，土靈，火靈），同時最多存在五個靈魂。
	所召喚的靈魂類型從薩滿當前等級可召喚的所有靈魂中隨機選擇。舉例來說，12級的薩滿可以召喚出一個小型自然靈，一個大型動物靈，又或一個小型動物靈，無法決定召喚出哪一種。召喚出的靈魂會盡他們所能去保護薩滿，但並不能直接控制它們。

職業限制：

–無法通過高感知來增加每天施法次數
–陣營限制為中立善良、絕對中立和中立邪惡
–無法獲得任何據點》~

@103063 = ~Spirit Ward
(Abjuration)

Level: 1
Sphere: Wards
Range: Touch
Duration: 3 rounds/level
Casting Time: 1
Area of Effect: 1 creature
Saving Throw: None

This spell surrounds the recipient with a magical barrier at a distance of one foot. Spirits, fey creatures, elementals, and spectral undead receive a penalty of -2 to hit when attacking the protected creature. In addition, the recipient gains a +3 bonus to Saving Throws against all spells that belong to the Enchantment school. This spell cannot be cast on spirits, fey creatures, elementals, or spectral undead.《靈魂守護
（防護系）

等級：1
領域：防護
距離：觸碰
持續時間：3輪/等級
施法時間：1
有效範圍：1個生物
豁免檢定：無

該法術在圍繞受術者1呎遠的地方產生一個魔法護罩。靈魂，精化生物，元素，以及鬼魂系不死生物在攻擊受保護生物時命中-2不利。此外，受術者在對所有附魔系法術進行豁免時+3有利。該法術無法對靈魂，精化生物，元素，以及鬼魂系不死生物施展。》~
@103064 = ~Favored of the Spirits《靈魂庇佑》~
@103065 = ~Favored of the Spirits

Range: 0
Duration: 1 hour
Casting Time: 9
Area of Effect: The caster
Saving Throw: None

This powerful rite shields the Shaman from death for 1 hour or until discharged. While under the protection of this rite, the Shaman is immune to all forms of death magic. In addition, if the Shaman is reduced below 10% Hit Points and the rite is active, the Shaman instantly receives the benefit of a Heal spell. The rite's protection (including the immunity to death) is completely discharged once the Heal spell is triggered.

Requires: Spirit Form《靈魂庇佑

距離：0
持續時間：5回合
施法時間：9
有效範圍：施法者
豁免檢定：無

這強大的儀式讓薩滿獲得對死亡的防護，持續10回合或直到被驅散為止。在儀式的保護下，薩滿對所有形式的死亡法術免疫。此外，如果薩滿的生命值降到10%以下且儀式依然有效，薩滿會立刻受到治療術的作用。一旦治療術觸發，則儀式的防護作用（包括對死亡的免疫）就會完全失效。

需要：靈魂形態》~

(Conjuration)

Level: 2
Sphere: Summoning
Range: Visual range of the caster
Duration: 1 turn
Casting Time: 2
Area of Effect: 15-ft. radius
Saving Throw: Special

This spell conjures a cloud of writhing fog that chills and hinders anyone within its area other than the caster. Creatures in the fog take 1d3 points of cold damage per round. In addition, there is a 20% chance that they must save vs. Death or be slowed for 1 round. Creatures immune to cold damage do not suffer any adverse effects from this spell.《痛苦迷霧
（咒法系）

等級：2

距離：施法者視線所及
持續時間：1回合
施法時間：2
有效範圍：半徑30呎
豁免檢定：特殊

該法術召喚出一團翻滾的迷霧，冰凍並妨礙有效範圍內除施法者之外的所有對象。雲霧中的生物每輪受到1d3寒冷傷害，此外，他們還有20%概率需要對死亡進行豁免檢定，失敗則減速1回合。對寒冷傷害免疫的生物不會受到該法術的任何不利影響。》~

@103071 = ~Spirit Fire《靈魂火焰》~
@103072 = ~Spirit Fire
(Conjuration)

Level: 4
Sphere: Summoning
Range: 40 ft. 
Duration: Instant 
Casting Time: 4
Area of Effect: 15-ft. radius 
Saving Throw: Special

As the Shaman casts this spell, energies gather together from the spirit world and form a pale blue sphere. The Shaman can throw the sphere so that it explodes into a burst of ghostly, azure flames, which deliver 1d4 points of magic damage per level of the Shaman (up to a maximum of 10d4). There is also a 33% chance that every enemy within the area of effect will be afflicted by the Doom spell (-2 penalty to Saving Throws and attack rolls for 1 turn). A successful Save vs. Spell halves the damage and negates the Doom effect. Spirits, fey creatures, elementals, and spectral undead take double damage.《靈魂火焰
（咒法系）

等級：4
領域：召喚
距離：40呎
持續時間：立即
施法時間：4
有效範圍：半徑30呎
豁免檢定：特殊

當薩滿施展這個法術的時候，來自靈魂世界的能量集中起來形成一個淡藍色的球體。薩滿能夠把球體扔出去，爆炸成一片鬼魅般的碧藍火焰，造成每個薩滿等級1d4點的魔法傷害（最高到10d4）。此外，法術有效範圍內的敵人還有33%的概率受到災難術的影響（在1回合內豁免和命中-2不利）。成功通過對法術的豁免檢定能夠使傷害減半並免受災難術的影響。靈魂，精化生物，元素，以及鬼魂系不死生物受到雙倍的傷害。》~

@103075 = ~Spiritual Lock《靈魂封鎖》~
@103076 = ~Spiritual Lock
(Enchantment)

Level: 6
Sphere: Wards
Range: 40 ft.
Duration: 1 turn + 1 round/level
Casting Time: 6
Area of Effect: 1 creature
Saving Throw: Negates

The target of Spiritual Lock must Save vs. Spell with a -2 penalty or have its mind temporarily sealed away within the spirit world. During this time, the victim is unable to perform any actions that require conscious thought such as attacking, using items, or casting spells. Spirits, fey creatures, elementals, and spectral undead Save vs. Spell with a -4 penalty instead of -2. Spiritual Lock is blocked by spells and abilities that protect against feeblemind effects.《靈魂封鎖
（附魔系）

等級：6
領域：防護
距離：40呎
持續時間：1回合+1輪/等級
施法時間：6
有效範圍：1個生物
豁免檢定：通過則無效

靈魂封鎖的目標必須以-2不利對法術進行豁免檢定，失敗則意識暫時被封印在靈魂世界。在此期間，受術者無法進行有意識的活動例如攻擊、使用物品或施展法術。靈魂，精化生物，元素，以及鬼魂系不死生物需要以-4而不是-2不利進行豁免檢定。靈魂封鎖會被對弱智效果進行防護的法術和能力所阻擋。》~

@103078 = ~Ether Gate《以太之門》~
@103079 = ~Ether Gate
(Alteration)

Level: 7
Sphere: Travelers
Range: Touch 
Duration: 5 rounds
Casting Time: 3
Area of Effect: 1 creature
Saving Throw: None

This spell transports one creature, chosen by the caster, to the Ethereal Plane. The creature vanishes for the spell's duration, at which point it returns to the physical world in the exact same spot where it was before. While in the Ethereal Plane, the victim cannot interact with anyone or anything that resides on the Prime Material Plane. There is no saving throw against this spell, though it is subject to magic resistance. Friendly creatures can lower their magic resistance so that the shaman can target them with this spell. In addition, Ether Gate is blocked by spells and abilities that protect against maze effects.《以太之門
（改變系）

等級：7
領域：旅行
距離：碰觸
持續時間：5輪
施法時間：3
有效範圍：1個生物
豁免檢定：無

該法術把施法者選定的一個生物傳送到以太位面。該生物在法術有效期間消失不見，然後會回到他之前所在的位置。當位於以太位面中時，受術者無法與主物質位面的任何人物或物品進行互動。該法術不需要進行豁免檢定，但仍然會受到法術抗力的影響。友好的生物會主動降低法術抗力從而薩滿能夠順利對他們施展法術。此外，以太之門會被免疫迷宮效果的法術和能力所阻擋。》~

Sphere: Summoning

@103096 = ~Dulf Ebonbeard

@103194 = ~Orc
Orcs are the hereditary enemies of goblins and hobgoblins, with whom they often compete for resources. Reasonably intelligent carnivores, orcs are constantly waging war against other races to maintain their tribes. These wars thin the weak predators from their tribes and gather resources for the next generation. Orcs have a reputation for being extremely powerful warriors. Wizards have tried to create orcish variants to take advantage of the race's natural ferocity and strength.《獸人
獸人是地精和大地精與生俱來的敵人，它們之間經常為了資源而競爭。作為具備一定智能的獵食者，獸人經常對其它種族發動戰爭以維持它們的部族。這些戰爭從它們的部族中把弱者消耗掉，並為下一代聚積資源。獸人以異常強大的戰士而聞名。巫師們曾經試著創造獸人的變種以利用這個種族的力量與兇猛。》~

@103219 = ~
The Polish translation of Baldur's Gate II: Enhanced Edition is based on the original translation done by CDProjekt, with additional texts introduced by Beamdog in the Enhanced Edition and translated by a team of volunteers and long-time BG Saga fans.

Baldur's Gate 2: Enhanced Edition is undoubtedly one of the biggest non-profit computer game translations done by volunteers, hobbyists and BG saga buffs. The whole project contains over 100 000 dialog lines and even if most of them come from the original version, there are still over 29 000 lines that needed to be translated from scratch. For comparison, a whole official add-on called Tales of the Sword Coast has 28 000 dialog lines.

Our interference in the original translation of Baldur's Gate II: Shadows of Amn, originally done by CDProjekt, was smaller than for Baldur's Gate: Enhanced Edition, because it became a base of Forgotten Realms and Dungeons & Dragons related terms for us. For example, for an infamous “Underdark” we have employed a commonly used translation “Podmrok” instead of “Świat Mroku”, that was used for the original BG1 translation. Nevertheless, we have still made countless of small corrections, both lingual and factual, and also unified all item, spell and innate abilities' description for the BGEE and BG2EE standard introduced by a Beamdog team.

Unexpected difficulty came with the translation of the additional adventure called “The Black Pits 2: Gladiators of Thay”. For “The Black Pits” we went with “Kręgi Podmroku”, but the name was not fit for the second installment, where the plot is taking place on the infamous arenas of Thay. Thus, we have decided to translate the title as “Kręgi Thay”, to allude to the first part of the adventure.

The Baldur's Gate 2: Enhanced Edition Polish Translation Team would like to thank members of the Children of Bhaal clan, especially to morgan for providing many fixes and corrections of the original BG2 translation and invaluable content-related and linguistic support and to Cuttooth for creating a fantastic little piece of software called FRTrans, a glossary of Forgotten Realms and Dungeons & Dragons related terms, which became a great help during translation and proofreading. Without their contribution our BG2EE translation would not be as it is today. Once again, kudos to you!《The Polish translation of Baldur's Gate II: Enhanced Edition is based on the original translation done by CDProjekt, with additional texts introduced by Beamdog in the Enhanced Edition and translated by a team of volunteers and long-time BG Saga fans.

Baldur's Gate 2: Enhanced Edition is undoubtedly one of the biggest non-profit computer game translations done by volunteers, hobbyists and BG saga buffs. The whole project contains over 100 000 dialog lines and even if most of them come from the original version, there are still over 29 000 lines that needed to be translated from scratch. For comparison, a whole official add-on called Tales of the Sword Coast has 28 000 dialog lines.

Our interference in the original translation of Baldur's Gate II: Shadows of Amn, originally done by CDProjekt, was smaller than for Baldur's Gate: Enhanced Edition, because it became a base of Forgotten Realms and Dungeons & Dragons related terms for us. For example, for an infamous 「Underdark」 we have employed a commonly used translation 「Podmrok」 instead of 「Świat Mroku」, that was used for the original BG1 translation. Nevertheless, we have still made countless of small corrections, both lingual and factual, and also unified all item, spell and innate abilities' description for the BGEE and BG2EE standard introduced by a Beamdog team.

Unexpected difficulty came with the translation of the additional adventure called 「The Black Pits 2: Gladiators of Thay」. For 「The Black Pits」 we went with 「Kręgi Podmroku」, but the name was not fit for the second installment, where the plot is taking place on the infamous arenas of Thay. Thus, we have decided to translate the title as 「Kręgi Thay」, to allude to the first part of the adventure.

The Baldur's Gate 2: Enhanced Edition Polish Translation Team would like to thank members of the Children of Bhaal clan, especially to morgan for providing many fixes and corrections of the original BG2 translation and invaluable content-related and linguistic support and to Cuttooth for creating a fantastic little piece of software called FRTrans, a glossary of Forgotten Realms and Dungeons & Dragons related terms, which became a great help during translation and proofreading. Without their contribution our BG2EE translation would not be as it is today. Once again, kudos to you!》~

@103221 = ~priest of Tempus《坦帕斯牧師》~
@103222 = ~Priest of Tempus《坦帕斯牧師》~
@103223 = ~PRIEST OF TEMPUS: Tempus, also known as the Lord of Battles or the Foehammer, is random in his favors, yet his chaotic nature favors all sides equally. Lord Tempus may be on an army's side one day and against them the next; such is the nature of war. Tempuran clergy can be found on both sides of a conflict, as none can ever truly know whom the war god will favor.

Advantages:
- May cast Holy Power once per day. Gains one use at level 1 and an additional use every 5 levels thereafter.
- May cast Chaos of Battle once per day. Gains one use at level 1 and an additional use every 10 levels thereafter.

CHAOS OF BATTLE: Chaos of Battle applies bonuses to all allies and penalties to all enemies within a 30-ft. radius of the caster. The spell lasts 1 turn and will randomly affect the targets' Armor Class, Hit Points, THAC0, saves, or luck. The magnitude of the effect starts at 1 (5 for Hit Points) at level 1 and will improve by 1 (5 for Hit Points) every 6 levels of the caster.

Disadvantages:
– Alignment restricted to chaotic good, chaotic neutral, chaotic evil, or true neutral.《坦帕斯牧師：坦帕斯，也被稱為「戰爭之王」或「仇敵之錘」，他的幫助是隨機的，然而他混亂的本性對各方都是平等的。坦帕斯今天可能與一支軍隊為友，明天可能就會與之為敵，或許這就是戰爭的本質。在衝突的雙方都可以找到信仰坦帕斯的神職人員，因為沒有人能真正知道誰是戰神會喜歡的人。

職業優勢：
－1級時每天可施展1次神聖之力，之後每5級每天可施展的次數+1
－1級時每天可施展1次混沌戰爭，之後每10級每天可施展的次數+1

混沌戰爭：
混沌戰爭可以30尺範圍內的給所有友方生物一個增益效果，而敵人將受到一個不利效果的影響。效果可持續一回合，但具體的效果是完全隨機的，包括：護甲等級、生命值、零級命中值、豁免以及幸運。影響的數值在牧師1級時為1（生命值受影響的數值為5），之後每6級+1（生命值為5）。

職業限制：
－必須是混亂善良、混亂中立、混亂邪惡或是絕對中立陣營》~

@103225 = ~Chaos of Battle

Chaos of Battle applies bonuses to all allies and penalties to all enemies within a 30-ft. radius of the caster. The spell lasts 1 turn and will randomly affect the targets' Armor Class, Hit Points, THAC0, saves, or luck. The magnitude of the effect starts at 1 (5 for Hit Points) at level 1 and will improve by 1 (5 for Hit Points) every 6 levels of the caster.《混沌戰爭
